**----- Start of picture text -----**<br>
ae mare Baker ge TE tay gia nee ot iat ee ae ot ;<br>oe) 2c ee a RS ae a<br>**----- End of picture text -----**<br>


The Umbra can be a dangerous place fora tiny Gaffling or even a Jaggling with no friends. Many spirits prefer independence and remain unaligned; but many others seek the patronage of an Incarna. Even some lesser Incarna recognize the safety of numbers, and therefore ally themselves with even stronger spirits. It is in this manner that the great Tribal Totems have accumulated many followers over the millennia. 

Each of the great totems is served by a host of spirits. Some are mighty Jagglings or even lesser Incarna; others are collections of Gafflings spawned directly from the totem itself. The following spirits by no means present the entirety of the Broods of the Totems, but are a representative sample of what spirits Garou might be likely to encounter in their Tribal Totem’s service. As with all 

spirits, these broods can prove to be invaluable allies — and as with all spirits, the price they exact can be more — than a Garou is willing to pay. 

Some spirit terminology may seem a bit confusing. For example, Rat is served by Rat Gafflings, while Stag com— mands Yale’s obedience. Yale serves Stay, yet a Garou could hardly bind Yale himself into a fetish. For simplicity’s sake, assume that any singular spirits referred to are freewilled, more powerful Jagglings or even lesser Incarna. (In such a case, it is far easier to bind a Gaffling avatar of the spirit than the spirit itself.) Similarly, if “Mosquito-spirits are mentioned, they are most likely common Geafflings. 

A number of spirits have access to new Charms; these can be found in the Appendix. New Charms are marked with an asterisk.
